commit d4aa8c246e207199a8b4fedbf6ee5f352a842290
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Fri Apr 8 18:11:34 2022 +0200

    Fix support for RTL layouts
    
    Make sure this app is never layed out from right-to-left because
    (shader) code is always layed out left-to-right. Also, there's no
    translation for a RTL language at the moment, so this kind of
    layout isn't helpful.
    
    If `supportsRtl` is set to `true`, white spaces are right-aligned
    and the caret positioning is off.
    
    For details see this issue:
    https://github.com/markusfisch/ShaderEditor/issues/111
    
    Thanks to @Mehran7kl for fixing this bug!

1	1	app/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml

commit 2881b2a1a25236eb7c1c4df1ae28c994da35e4b4
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Tue Mar 1 21:16:40 2022 +0100

    Automatically convert ShaderToy sources
    
    This has been requested several times, although I see relatively
    little benefit in it.
    
    ShaderToy is hardly usable on a mobile phone. For example, I can't
    even copy the source code of a shader because the JavaScript won't
    let me. Also, this app only supports a small subset of ShaderToy's
    uniforms. So most of the shaders can't be converted anyway.
    
    Let's see if this really has any value for anybody.

commit 0204f904809572a29d36773b9c6c84d2c4e35cd4
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Wed Jan 26 20:24:28 2022 +0100

    Ignore lint warning about the custom splash screen
    
    Androidx SplashScreen compat library would require minSdk 21,
    make the app unnecessarily larger and Android 12 automatically
    replaces our custom splash screen anyway, which is exactly what
    we want. So there is no reason to complain.
    
    The migration guide says about our kind of splash screen:
    
    > If your existing splash screen is implemented using a custom
    > theme that overrides android:windowBackground, the system replaces
    > your custom splash screen with a default Android system splash
    > screen on Android 12 and higher (which may not be your app’s
    > intended experience).
    
    Source:
    https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/ui/splash-screen/migrate
    
    This is not only the intended but desired experience for this app.

8	0	app/lint.xml

commit 3068fd4f73555bdfb01512019efae2698f7ddc5b
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Thu Dec 16 20:45:28 2021 +0100

    Remove checking URL intent with resolveActivity()
    
    Because of the new package visibility restrictions in API level 30+,
    we can no longer use `resolveActivity()` to check if we can run
    `startActivity()` with a given `Intent` (in this case opening a URL).
    
    Instead, we should simply try and catch the `ActivityNotFoundException`.

commit 911e6e15d987f60a06ff954aa5aad04df52580bb
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Tue Oct 19 21:07:56 2021 +0200

    Remove listening for ACTION_POWER_*
    
    Overlaps with ACTION_BATTERY_CHANGED.
    
    The only difference is that ACTION_POWER_* will wake the app when
    ACTION_BATTERY_CHANGED does not. Since these events are only important
    when this app is awake (including when the live wallpaper is running),
    it's better to not wake up on ACTION_POWER_* broadcasts and keep
    sleeping ;)

commit 4bab8466df5574f04db720175a2cd1ebb4fc4e97

Date:   Sat Nov 9 18:52:15 2019 +0100

    Remove update listener to set async loaded bitmap
    
    That was over-thinking a problem that doesn't really exist
    and introducing a memory leak along the way.
    
    The static UpdateListener held a reference to the latest
    Fragment object that couldn't be garbage collected because
    of it. Rookie mistake.

commit 491d060e5635bd691100f6a148f02d75bd3865b3
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Thu Nov 7 23:57:52 2019 +0100

    Fix undo/redo to ignore initial change
    
    Because the editor (usually) doesn't start blank but with some source
    in it. We don't want to undo before that inital change. Otherwise it
    would be possible to undo before the source was loaded and end up with
    a blank editor.
    
    This requires some very specific modifications to the original
    implemenation (fi.iki.asb.android.logo.TextViewUndoRedo) because of
    which I moved this class into the main namespace and matched its style
    with the rest of the source.
    
    Also, the undo/redo history can now be outside of the UndoRedo class.
    I did this to make it static and to not put extra load on configuration
    (read orientation) changes as the original implemenation would have
    done (because it saves/restores the history with shared preferences).
    
    A downside of this is that the history is lost as soon as the app is
    killed now. I still prefer to have fast configuration changes.

commit ec60e66b6fceebc90709ea94f4c10d198cc4e2e6
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Feb 3 12:40:39 2019 +0100

    Add uniform for Sensor.TYPE_ROTATION_VECTOR
    
    Because the rotation matrix (and thus the device orientation)
    can be calculated approximately from the rotation vector using
    SensorManager.getRotationMatrixFromVector().
    
    This may come in handy when TYPE_MAGNETIC_FIELD isn't available
    what is required for Sensor.getRotationMatrix().

commit 3a1df1715076b38009313ca10ecb0e67054c36f9
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Mon Jan 8 20:02:18 2018 +0100

    Add uniform for frame count
    
    As requested.
    
    Please note, a signed integer in medium precision has only
    a guaranteed minimum range of 2^15. This means, rendering
    at 60 frames per second, that the counter may wrap after
    32768 / 60 = ~546 seconds or ~9 minutes.

commit 891029c649066dbed723743cdb390dbf55427f98
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Apr 29 17:23:58 2018 +0200

    Suppress static leak lint warning for AsyncTasks
    
    See, those AsyncTasks are *meant* to keep their parent instance
    around while they're running. There's nothing wrong with keeping
    the instance for a short while.
    
    If you think different, consider if it's really worth the extra
    complexity of introducing a weak reference or a bus system or
    something similar. Would that make things better or just fat?
    Would that "better" even be noticeable?

commit 7f5c3d0533b0dbc4ad88a84a0062d5598e48f25a
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Apr 15 22:12:46 2018 +0200

    Release camera when opening is cancelled
    
    Since the camera is opened in a background thread, it may
    happen that the Activity enters onPause() before or while
    the opening is in process. For example, this may happen
    when there are a couple of quick orientation changes.
    
    So make sure every opened camera object is properly closed.
    
    Also better use a shortcut for the camera member variable
    to avoid confusion with function parameters.

commit 257c5f9be078f0c6d61f3043c37d41b11886b790
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Feb 25 18:47:37 2018 +0100

    Use ACCELEROMETER if GRAVITY/LA isn't available
    
    TYPE_GRAVITY and TYPE_LINEAR_ACCELERATION seem not be available
    on all devices. Got a beta feedback from a user on a Samsung Galaxy
    J2 saying that gravity and linear uniforms no longer are working
    after changing to TYPE_GRAVITY and TYPE_LINEAR_ACCELERATION.
    
    So if the app can't register one of these (software) sensors,
    it'll fallback to use TYPE_ACCELEROMETER and calculate linear
    and gravity from that (as before).

    Use GLES 3.0 if available

    to declare that version with the line "#version 300 es".
    
    The app will automatically pick a version 3 vertex shader
    if that declaration is present AND GLES 3.0 is available.

commit d0d609e030d1c5c160106811b73ed336327e1038
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Mon Aug 14 22:50:37 2017 +0200

    Set an initial backbuffer texture
    
    Use the texture parameter comment like this:
    
            uniform sampler2D backbuffer;///p:noise
    
    Where `noise` is the name of the texture.
    Can be combined with all the other texture parameters.

commit 004b31933ee982f2b4471c67f62181fc554e47ec
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Tue Aug 8 23:07:32 2017 +0200

    Made TabWidthSpan static to not leak memory
    
    What a silly mistake ... TabWidthSpan wasn't static so it
    kept a reference to its parent instance, the View, which
    in turn has a reference to its Activity. And so neither
    the View nor the Activity can get ever released.

commit 9dd8e1af7517e11784c84cc2251a619839af7edd
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Wed May 3 21:57:03 2017 +0200

    Support custom texture parameters for each sampler
    
    Use something like "///min:n;mag:l;s:c;t:c" after a sampler2D or
    samplerCube to set parameters for glTexParameteri(). This way each
    shader can define custom parameters for each sampler.
    
    Also there's a widget to choose from the possible values when a
    new texture is added or inserted into the source.

commit 28cddcd0298984fcfa179bff42a4d6b0b321bb86
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Mon Mar 13 21:10:40 2017 +0100

    Don't check findViewById() return values for null
    
    Given we test every change, findViewById() can only return null
    in development but not in production. Once the wiring is correct,
    findViewById() cannot fail.
    
    Even worse, if findViewById() returns null because we make a
    mistake while developing, there won't be a telling exception if
    we check for null and just finish the activity.

commit b03d6b8b739586afcea0bd34d3d0a84c14eea098
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Fri Mar 3 23:10:47 2017 +0100

    Don't transfer shader query over config changes
    
    Don't keep a static (hard) reference to the latest Activity object
    because that would keep the GC from recycling it long after its
    use. Of course, it'd be possible to use a WeakReference and avoid
    leaking that Activity, but there's really no point in worrying
    about having a new configuration querying shaders again.

commit 6fa8f63c8cb16778c2629b35f4b92e1277e0c4ce
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Fri Jan 6 17:52:30 2017 +0100

    Transfer delayed results from background tasks
    
    Into the currently active UI object. When a device is rotated
    while an AsyncTask is running, the result of that AsyncTask
    should be transferred to the new Activity/Fragment.
    
    The simplest way to do this is to use a static reference to
    a private listener that is initialized in onCreate/View().
    Since AsyncTask.onPostExectue() and onCreate()/onCreateView()
    are both running on the main thread, they can never overlap
    and the result is always realized in the latest active object.

commit 07374533e822c81ada3f70c1dd7b33a6cde5dcc3
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Oct 2 18:23:40 2016 +0200

    Restored ScrollView around EditText
    
    Yes, TextView can scroll already, but it's not possible to set a
    padding on it's contents only. Instead, contents will be cut off
    at the specified padding but before the visible border leaving
    an ugly gap between text and border.
    
    The only way to avoid this seems to be putting the TextView inside
    a ScrollView.

commit ea6d60237e8135946cde06c4d00fd57d43379e6d
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Oct 2 14:12:42 2016 +0200

    Don't keep a reference to Context in DataSource
    
    Lint complains because keeping a Context in a static place usually
    leads to a memory leak. In this case, however, context was the
    application context (which never gets garbage collected anyway).
    
    Because it'd leave a bad smell, the reference was removed.

commit e7c44b1da1344097e6d80487364bb8889fac648b
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Sep 4 14:45:36 2016 +0200

    Set current shader as wallpaper shader
    
    Change the current wallpaper shader from inside the app.
    If the current shader is the wallpaper shader, the menu
    item will say "Update wallpaper". Otherwise it will read
    "Set as wallpaper".
    
    Note that this only works if Shader Editor is already set
    as live wallpaper. Android doesn't allow apps to set a
    live wallpaper directly (so we'd need to fire an intent
    for the wallpaper chooser; but that's probably too much).

commit 7291522828198da79ade493b5daf3d2bd155005d
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Wed Aug 31 19:39:37 2016 +0200

    New setting to open preview activity in new task
    
    Since FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK cannot be combined with
    startActivityForResult(), see
    
    https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK
    
      "This flag can not be used when the caller is requesting
       a result from the activity being launched."
    
    and because FLAG_ACTIVITY_LAUNCH_ADJACENT does nothing
    without FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK and FLAG_ACTIVITY_NEW_TASK
    causes multiple preview activities < Nougat, it's probably
    best to have a dedicated setting for this.
    
    So if you want support for Nougat's multi-window mode, you
    need to choose "Run as a new task" in Settings -> Run Mode.

commit 90d649dffebf4c6d8bf4153638995fa7e6599b8d
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Fri Aug 19 16:00:43 2016 +0200

    New second and subsecond uniform, changed ftime
    
    To better cope with mediump float precision limitations,
    there are two new uniforms: int second and float subsecond.
    subsecond contains only the fractional part of the seconds
    since start.
    
    ftime ranges between -1.0 and +1.0 and wraps every PI seconds
    now. This gives mediump devices a couple of opportunities to
    avoid rounding errors.

3	1	app/src/main/res/values/strings.xml

commit fb61f0da84c866e81f3c36ad87fd97579ba2c83a
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Fri Aug 19 13:30:27 2016 +0200

    Extra uniform to transfer fractional part of time
    
    Since precision problems of a mediump float (time) arise
    quite early. Transferring just the fractional part gives
    more precision because the precision limitation for decimals
    between -1.0 and +1.0 are much lower than with higher
    decimals.

commit 9dccc72157ebaf77a1b4a8ddc3b710efea665104
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Thu Mar 3 22:47:16 2016 +0100

    Added note about returning a mutable reference
    
    The thumbnail is generated on the fly on the drawing thread.
    The data doesn't need to be protected from modification and
    doing so (by copying) would only mean to use more memory
    than necessary.

Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Mon Feb 29 22:53:03 2016 +0100

    Make static members of application context final
    
    Declaring the static members of the application context as
    final is syntactically better because those members will
    never change. The only reason they weren't final was, that
    I preferred to make the objects only constructable with a
    context object. Switched to late initialization because
    it's probably more important to have the static members
    to be final.

commit 5d9a5a4cb952d87eacf9d9a69f2eed3e6f564451
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Feb 21 15:42:25 2016 +0100

    Add READ_EXTERNAL_STORAGE permission for API < 19
    
    Required to import textures on API < 19 from gallery apps
    that do not use grantUriPermission(). Later API's will not
    see that permission.
    
    Hard decision. I don't really want to add that permission
    but people (on API's < 19, especially Samsung devices)
    keep running into this limitation and I just don't see a
    better way to fix this.
    
    At the time of writing, about 25% of installs will be
    affected by this and will need to manually confirm the
    update containing this change.

commit 7399fd5ca168b1b146ee7b72d3de6e397fd192b8
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Thu Jan 7 19:07:46 2016 +0100

    Transparent background color in error highlighting
    
    Because EditText draws the cursor before the background of
    Spannables, an opaque background color will make the cursor
    disappear. There's an issue about that:
    
    https://code.google.com/p/android/issues/detail?id=172001
    
    For the time being, the simplest solution is to make the
    background color transparent. It may not be as eye-catching
    as before but it's probably still good enough to clearly see
    where the error is.

    Drop glClear() to preserve pixel buffer

    should not update the buffer. So glClear() needs to be dropped because
    it clears the buffer between renders.

commit 33a2dc37e5fb66ef26e5273098ab1b4ca56e6266
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Mon Dec 7 18:19:44 2015 +0100

    Removed infer rule
    
    Unfortunately, Infer isn't quite there yet.
    
    It's a pain to install (compliation breaks with 0.4.0) and
    (at least 0.2.0) can't see if you're closing a cursor in a
    method and not in the current context:
    
            Cursor cursor = ...
    
            if( closeIfEmpty( cursor ) )
                    return;
    
    You can close the cursor in closeIfEmpty() but that won't
    keep Infer from complaining. There are other situations
    like when you're putting a cursor into an adapter that
    trigger the same kind of warning altough you're calling
    adapter.changeCursor( null ); to close it.
    
    Looking for other static analysis tools.

commit 3cfa2d38e81391f907e7dbd698b8d09c368ef358
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sat Dec 5 21:49:39 2015 +0100

    Catch security exception when choosing an image
    
    Content providers that do no grant permission for the transferred
    image URI will cause a security exception. Samsung's image gallery
    on the Galaxy Note 2 is such a bad example.
    
    Since all other gallery apps I've tried so far (not too many) do
    grant the permission, I chose to add a toast informing the user
    to use another gallery app to pick the image.
    
    If this problem has a broader scope, there's no way around
    READ_EXTERNAL_STORAGE what I would like to avoid because it's
    a "dangerous permission" on Marshmallow and it's simply not
    really required.

    Removed unused texture file path option

    Moved settings from drawer into menu
    
    It's probably a bit confusing having settings in the
    drawer at the left (start) and the rest of the options
    in the overflow menu at the right (end).

    becomes quite small on small screens or landscape with
    additional menu items in the drawer.
    
    After trying the textures menu item in the drawer, it
    became quite clear, that the drawer should only contain
    the list of shaders and nothing else.

commit 6f278fb920072f85c6fc23a30724127b99333a7f
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Thu Sep 17 20:43:45 2015 +0200

    Restart rendering when the device is plugged in
    
    The docs are a bit unclear what BATTERY_OKAY really means.
    According to my tests, BATTERY_OKAY is not sent when the
    device is plugged in. Not even when the power level raised
    above BATTERY_LOW.
    
    So it's probably a good idea to listen for
    ACTION_POWER_CONNECTED too.

commit 0056b931636b8d061c751bc49bd0bc0ab4391118
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Aug 16 22:22:47 2015 +0200

    Wrap time variable
    
    Time holds the number of milliseconds since the creation of the
    OpenGL surface. This number can get quickly very big what pretty
    soon will result in rounding errors because a mediump float is
    not very long.
    
    When that happens, results from calculations that rest on the
    uniformity of the time variable will jump. The animation stutters.
    
    To avoid this, the time variable wraps early now.

5	2	ShaderEditor/src/main/java/de/markusfisch/android/shadereditor/opengl/ShaderRenderer.java

commit 82ed68b1e6482eb6802d359ff95a025ba8f38a1a
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Mar 22 16:37:13 2015 +0100

    Bind texture again for drawing into framebuffer
    
    Some drivers (e.g. on the Fairphone 1) require binding
    the texture again after glDrawArrays() was called for
    some reason.
    
    Also removed the depth buffer of the framebuffer since
    it's completely unnecessary for what this app does.
    
    The backbuffer texture is cleared before use now.
    Some drivers start with uninitialized texture data.

commit 797e1313c90504b7b8e0d0071e6e12458a922d48
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sat Feb 28 16:28:42 2015 +0100

    Use fixed alpha for low pass filter
    
    Previous calculation was wrong. t is the low pass' filter
    time constant (!) and dT is the event delivery rate in nano
    seconds.
    
    Chose to use a constant for now (and to ignore delta time).

1	2	src/de/markusfisch/android/shadereditor/AccelerometerListener.java

commit 9339caa05257b603b9dbec43f147f3fd08616c99
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sat Feb 28 15:41:42 2015 +0100

    Fixed y-flipped rendering when using a frame buffer
    
    If the texture frame buffer (backbuffer) is rendered first,
    rendering to frame buffer 0 (the screen) next will result in
    a flipped image (on the y axis).
    
    Maybe that's because rendering into a texture is (by default?)
    y-flipped because a textures origin (0/0) is always in the
    bottom left. And maybe the transformation matrix does not get
    reset on glBindFramebuffer( GL_FRAMEBUFFER, 0 ).
    
    Anyway, rendering into frame buffer 0 first does fix the
    problem.

commit 726f2ad7aa958528daf9ce4bd96f2e21123c7fb1
Author: Markus Fisch <mf@markusfisch.de>
Date:   Sun Aug 11 14:18:45 2013 +0200

    Fixed resetting of soft keyboard
    
    At first, I don't need to call setText() to update the text. It's enough
    to change the Editable.
    
    TextView.setText() will restart the InputMethodManager which will reset
    the soft keyboard.
    
    Second, don't use Editable.clearSpans() as it will remove too much.
    Removing only the spans I added is enough.

    when the adapter changes which may update the spinner not immediately.

    and if fps did actually change so that shoudln't be problem
